  <a id="15246" class="Keyword">where</a>
  
  <a id="15257" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.cyclic-types.html#15257" class="Function">equiv-Cyclic</a> <a id="15270" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15272" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#222" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="15275" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15276" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.cyclic-types.html#15185" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="15279" href="Agda.Primitive.html#810" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="15281" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.cyclic-types.html#15188" class="Bound">l2</a><a id="15283" class="Symbol">)</a>
